2466|Tatooine: Mos Eisley||A Jedi's Plans (V)\par Master Kenobi (V)\par Mindful Of The Future\par Senator Mon Mothma (V)\par Tatooine: Cantina (V)\par Visored Vision (V)\par Yarna d'al' Gargan (V)|Tatooine: Mos Eisley|Tatooine: Mos Eisley + Tatooine: Cantina\par Keep the Dark Side troops away and Force drain while awaiting an opportune time to counter attack.\par -----\par If you're going to play with Tatooine sites, these are a must. Cantina is a 2/2 site and Mos Eisley lets you move to and from there for free during your control phase.\par So, stack your characters on one of those two sites to better withstand a battle, then on your control phase move some of them over to the other, drain at both, and then move the ones you didn't move yet to re-consolidate your forces.\par -----\par Tatooine: Mos Eisley + Spaceport Speeders\par Once you're there movement is free, so you don't need the speeder anymore.
